------

mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈景捷、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈新年、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">陈秀洁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、陈秀萍、陈雪清、陈岩、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陈艳群、</span>陈跃飞</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈鹰军、陈友荣、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈昱昊、陈玉花、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陈云飞</span>、陈泽奇、陈兆志、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程德亮、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程桂靖</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">程桂英</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、程进峰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程全云</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程西江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、程学珍、程渊、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程志春、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">次成加材（藏）、次成嘉措（藏）、次旺（藏）、次旺嘉措（藏）、仓央嘉措（藏）、赤列（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丛霞、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔斌、崔德（藏）、崔兰琴、崔永强、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡彩影：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东佛山市张槎小学英语教师、法轮功学员。蔡彩影在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月迫害法轮功以来，她曾多次被绑架迫害，曾经被非法判刑七年，家庭破碎。蔡彩影<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被抓捕，被关押在佛山看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月左右，蔡彩影被佛山市禅城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，目前被关押在广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡恒军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省辛集市法轮功学员。河北辛集市南智邱镇东陈家庄村人，在深圳给儿子看孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日中午一点左右，深圳市龙田派出所闯入蔡恒军儿子家中，将蔡恒军抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在广东深圳庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。现关押于河北保定市监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡俊平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南许昌市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，家住许昌市建安区苏桥镇蔡庄村，为人淳朴善良，踏实能干，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年初，他开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，许昌市建安区国保大队与苏桥镇派出所等多个警察，到苏桥镇蔡庄村蔡俊平的家，非法抄家，抄走计算机、打印机等私人物品，将蔡俊平抓捕关押到许昌市建安区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，蔡俊平被许昌市魏都区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在河南新密监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡林华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员蔡林华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡伟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，哈尔滨市法轮功学员。大学本科毕业，从事财务统计工作多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日过遭抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，蔡伟华被入黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡予华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省三门峡市法轮功学员，女，二零二一年四月左右被判刑四年半，现已被劫持到河南省新乡女子监狱。蔡予华由于坚定修炼法轮功，在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年前被中共劳教（具体时间不详）。蔡予华由于在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向最高法院和检察院邮寄控告迫害元凶江泽民的控告信，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日晚上被抓捕、关押，家人被勒索财物，后又被判刑，在新乡女子监狱，受尽折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，蔡予华向有关部门邮寄了申诉控告信，要求返还并按时发放她在判刑期间被剥夺的养老保险金。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，蔡予华被三门峡陕州区警察从家中抓捕，关押在三门峡市看守所，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，后被送往新乡女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，长春市农安县法轮功学员，农民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨六点多钟，在农安县政府大楼对面，一群国保公安人员抓捕一家三口——蔡玉英、于娇茹母女，和这家老实巴交的男主人。那天，农安县非法抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。此次非法抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的，长春市政法委书记马延峰亲赴农安县部署非法抓捕行动，七月十三日，农安县政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”召开会议落实具体行动方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日判决书下到看守所：蔡玉英被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡智慧</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区法轮功学员，</span>蔡智慧在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被吉林警察抓捕到吉林省的看守所，后获悉其被吉林法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434767.html#211212222835-1"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434767.html#211212222835-1</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹爱兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，河南南阳油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年她修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，曹爱兰因为坚持信仰法轮大法，曾四次被绑架，两次判刑，累计陷冤狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局采取统一行动，在南阳地区开始绑架法轮功学员，两陷冤狱的法轮功学员曹爱兰老太被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曹爱兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹春生：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，河南省郑州市高新区石佛办事处百炉屯村大街<span lang="EN-US">159</span>号居民，私营塑料制品生产经营业主，抗暴维权者、中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月以来，其房屋一直被郑州市高新区石佛办事处政府威胁强拆，部分财产已遭损坏，出于无奈，自此其走上拆迁维权之路；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其住房在被镇政府暴力强拆时家人竟被打伤；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其所开办工厂再次遭当地政府强拆；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，一批手持各种器械及大型机械的强拆者欲将其剩余房屋进行野蛮强拆，为保护家园，其全家奋起反抗，双方随发生激烈冲突，混乱中为了自卫，其将对方其中二人刺伤，最终导致一死一伤，自己也在冲突中受伤，之后逃走；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其被郑州警方在三门峡市灵宝县以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”拘捕，并关押于郑州市第三看守所；另有一名远房亲戚也因其在逃亡中曾在他家待过而被警方以涉嫌“窝藏罪”刑拘；据悉，其与强拆方发生冲突时，有村民远距离拍下一些照片和证据，后来不幸均被警方没收销毁；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案被郑州市中牟县检察院起诉至郑州市中牟县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，终被郑州市中牟县法院以“故意伤害罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。目前在河南省焦南监狱（河南焦作市映湖路焦南监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">454003</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹进兴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，唐山市农机局退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在中共当局的“敲门行动”中，他被唐山市路北区文化路派出所警察绑架。警察非法抄家持续了三个小时，家中大量私人物品被抢劫。在警察绑架过程中，曹进兴被摔伤，缝了几针。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕，在唐山市第一看守所被关押一年多，后背生了很多皮疹。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，河北唐山市路北区一审判处曹进兴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曹三强</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：祖籍湖南，曾在当地创立家庭教会，是“中国福音会”牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年汶川地震后，曾从事四川基督教爱心工作，帮助学生及地震灾民度过难关。多年前，曹三强到云南普洱从事宣教、慈善救济及兴教办学事业，并在当地创办多所学校，帮助贫困儿童入学。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，他与基督徒景如霞从缅甸佤邦（缅甸第二特区）返国时，出于便利使用了非正式方式入境中国，被边防武警拦截拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日即被当地检察院以涉嫌“偷越国境罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日该案移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日该案在孟连县法院开庭，曹三强的亲友参加了旁听。尽管曹三强的辩护人刘培福律师认为，其当事人的行为不应构成犯罪，但他仍于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被云南省孟连县法院以“偷越国境罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元人民币，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。另一位基督徒景如霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，已当庭释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的曹三强牧师已转到位于云南省昆明市东郊王大桥的昆明监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹艳芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，五十多岁，吉林省榆树市法轮功学员。曹艳芬<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被吉林市船营区公安分局欢喜岭派出所警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年后，已被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柴茂荣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：云南昆明市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日柴茂荣在昆明市官渡区关上街农贸市场买菜时被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>华检察院指控柴茂荣使用带有法轮功宣传口号的人民币购物，并在包内有带有法轮功宣传口号的人民币以及护身符卡片等，在家中有法轮功宣传品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，柴茂荣被五华法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹永亮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，县人，山西省汾西县永安镇郭村村民，职业不详，维权人士，中国在押维权人士。曾因汾西县政府在炸无证黑煤窑时，将住宅房屋震塌，且无人赔偿，自此走上维权上访之路，期间曾多次遭遇拘留，其户口本亦因累次上访而被警方恶意没收；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因在京上访时遭截访、欺骗和毒打等迫害，地方当局先是答应给其赔偿<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元，并当场支付现金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，打欠条<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，但将其带到北京市长安西街派出所后，即遭警方毒和搜身，致其后来长期身体虚弱、吐血不止、大小便流血，其刚拿到的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元赔偿金亦被抢走、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元欠条被撕毁，随后被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因继续上访又被右安门派出所警方毒打，并被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；此后，再次因上访而被拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，且每次都是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，当其在北京打工之时，被前来的汾西县警方突然抓回老家，遭毒打后被关至临汾市尧都区吴村看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，即被汾西县警方以“伪造居民身份证、寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被汾西县检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被山西省汾西县法院以“伪造身份证罪、寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；据悉，看守所关押期间，屡受非人折磨，曾被毒打导致其头破血流，眼睛看不见，眉骨骨折；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刑满获释；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，山西省汾西县当局因惧怕其在“百年党庆”时期再到北京上访，影响党国形象，随指派当地警方为其提供生活困难补助<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，以令其立刻中止去京上访；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其认为中共“百年党庆”敏感期已过，遂就到国家信访局继续提交申诉材料，岂料<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在北京暂住地遭遇截访；遣回原籍之后，先是送山西省蒲县看守所被拒收，又于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被送乡宁县隔离，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个多月后，在其家人委托的律师努力打听下终于获知，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>日，其案被山西省汾西县法院庭审宣判，最终被以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前被羁押于山西省临汾市尧都区看守所<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常珈瑄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，山西省临汾市人，退役军人，临汾市尧都区解放西路<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号“常家大院”（祖宅）继承人之一，著名维权公民，维权致残者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年以来，因其从清代传承下来的祖宅曾被山西省晋南专区地方国营建筑工程队借走，历经数十载后，借方竟不想再谈归还之事，其父常耀文遂被迫携其全家人走上投诉维权之路<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年，其父带着妻儿数十人举家欲迁回祖宅居住，租房方不仅不如约归还，反以昔日领导“现在都管不了”为由久拖不给，其父无奈，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，随一纸诉状将临汾市建筑工程总公司告上地方法院；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，临汾市人民法院派人向当年的证人、中保等数人取证，经过比对，认为证词皆与常耀文所诉情况一致，所以于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，法院对其案双方进行了调解；不料被告方一边应诉，一边却仍与中国建行银行临汾市支行办理房屋交割手续，临汾市法院针此最终判定：“买卖无效，撤销其违法买卖涉及本案房产的有关手续”；被告方（又即借房方）不服，提起上诉，后经临汾市中级法院二审裁决：支持一审裁判；但借房方仍不服判决，反复几次提起上诉，而当地的政府土地部门亦对此事久拖<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不予裁定 ；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，因临汾市建筑工程总公司谎称“上世纪<span lang="EN-US">50</span>年代已购得<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号院，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年被常耀文占用并在此院内违法建筑，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年临汾市国土资源局确权该院国有土地使用权归属该公司”，并以此为由将其父枉法诬告上法庭，要求其父“停止侵权、恢复原状、返还财产”；此案件被受理后，尧都区法院一审以“原告起诉状中涉及的违法建筑应当由有关行政执法部门查处，不属于法院民事受案范围”，驳回了该借房公司的起诉；该公司仍然不服，再次上诉，又经临汾市中级法院终审裁定：一审的裁定驳回起诉正确；但遗憾的是，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其父常耀文未等来土地证即与世长辞。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其母再度委托律师、其及其姊常春枝，提出土地权属申请；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，临汾市国土资源局受理了该案件，但此后除<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次发出延期调查处理通知书之外，一直未予办结；其全家在维权诉讼过程中，曾屡遭殴打侮辱，导致其父受伤卧床不起，其被临汾市规划局打断四根肋骨，成了残疾人；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其姐弟二人相继被临汾市警方抓捕，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”、 “妨碍公务罪”指定居所监视居住；后被正式逮捕被羁押于临汾市尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，常珈瑄因抗强拆，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在山西晋城监狱二监区服刑。何时开庭何时宣判，一概不知。同时被捕的其姐常春枝怎样，目前情况不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玮平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西人权律师，原陕西立刚律师事务所律师。常玮平律师因为代理所谓敏感案件，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被停业</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月，及后原本的执业律师事务所被注销，需要在半年内转到其他律师楼继续执业，否则执照会被吊销。后他异地转所至浙江，也受到阻碍。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日常玮平律师到杭州市西湖区法院递交诉状，起诉浙江省司法厅不履行调转律师档案法定职责。常律师自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日向浙江省司法厅提交了转入浙江左契律师事务所的申请后，该厅迄今未办理。常玮平律师被迫处于被吊销律师执业证书的状态。常玮平律师因厦门公民聚会案于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日晚在西安住处被西安公安局高新区分局带走，办案单位是宝鸡市公安局高新区分，后常玮平的妻子接到宝鸡高新分局国保大队电话，被告知常玮平因危害国家安全，已经被指定居所监视居住。随后其律师执业证遭注销。后于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">21</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日取保获释回家。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月后，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日常玮平又遭指定居所监视居住。常玮平被再次抓捕的原因是他在海外网站上发布视频控诉其遭受的令人发指的酷刑，遭宝鸡警方挟私报复。后律师申请对其取保，遭宝鸡警方拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日）家属收到了常玮平的逮捕通知书，他已被关到了秦岭山中的凤县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男、<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，曾用名常玉光，陕西省西安市人，西安市高陵区泾渭上城小区<span lang="EN-US">41</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">1</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">3</span>层<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号公民，基督徒，陕西光义爱圣印务公司法人代表，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起，因其所属印务公司大量印刷了与基督教信仰有关的数据及图书，随引起地方当局的高度关注与警惕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，西安市文化执法部门联合西安市国家安全部门对其公司进行了查封与鉴定，现场扣押各种宗教类书籍<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万余册，后又经陕西省新闻出版和电影质量检测中心对其中《改革宗信仰》等<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书鉴定，认定该<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书为“未经批准擅自印刷的出版物”的非法出版物，随于次日（<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），立刻与其妻李琛慧被西安市高陵区警方一并抓走，后被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被更换罪名以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被西安市高陵区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其在无印刷许可证的情况下经营印刷业务，印刷非法出版物，扰乱市场秩序，起行为均构成非法经营罪，故而应予以逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被西安市高陵区法院一审以“非法经营罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，经陕西省西安市中级法院二审裁决，最终仍然驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。目前仍被羁押于西安市高陵区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑，暂不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/7.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/7.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈呈香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北监利访民李树南妻子。李树南：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省荆州市监利县白螺镇人，监利县白螺镇五里庙村村民，司法不公举报人，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李树南、陈呈香夫妇被荆州市监利县警方从家中突然带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，知其早已被转正式批捕，其案现已被检察院以同罪由移交至湖北省荆州市监利县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，李树南、陈呈香夫妻二人寻衅滋事案，在监利县检察院视频开庭，被告人大女儿李艳华，律师尚满庆、杨高华到达现场。在庭审过程中，检察官以其夫妻二人多次扰乱公共秩序、敲诈勒索予以定罪，建议给予<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年刑期。未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，李树南、陈呈香夫妇分别获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。目前二人均被羁押于荆州市监利县看守所。陈呈香刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">陈彩敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁省朝阳市凌源市小城子乡法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，凌源市小城子乡法轮功学员陈彩敏、李翠霞，在内蒙古赤峰市宁城县天义镇被天义派出所抓捕，天义派出所和凌源市小城子派出所对她们抄家，后被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午在宁城县法院第四法庭被开庭，二人均被判刑一年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/1/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-433112.html#211031225039-2"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/1/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-433112.html#211031225039-2</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈德芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被绑架到凌云宾馆铐在铁椅子上<span lang="EN-US">16</span>天，后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日送宝鸡市第二看守所非法刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给陈德芳下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈迪才：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，大学文化，户籍所在地是黄石市下辖阳新县黄颡口镇。<a name="_Hlk54957732"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚，他的姐姐被她丈夫李生水家暴殴打，外甥女打电话给舅舅陈迪才打电话，随后陈迪才骑车到姐家，看见姐姐被打得躺在床上，地上有被扯下的几缕头发。</a>陈迪才与姐夫李生水理论，李生水打电话举报陈迪才炼法轮功。晚十一点左右，黄石市黄石港区红旗桥派出所警察把陈迪才和她姐一家带到派出所，在陈迪才身上搜出几张真相币和含有法轮功内容的<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，派出所立即联系了黄石港区国保大队。陈迪才被关押、构陷一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被视频开庭，以捏造的「事实」判处陈迪才<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈法庆</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">浙江环保人士。<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，农民企业家出身。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年前，他曾经和江苏省环保人士吴立红自费在“纽约时报”刊登中英文环保公益广告，敦促当时刚上任的政治局常委，兑现环保承诺。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，陈法庆被当局以“组织领导传销活动”为由，刑事拘留。家属认为，该事件与中共十九大即将召开有关。家属称，陈法庆多年来不断受到当局打压，谋生遇到很多障碍。不到<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月前，他曾向习近平寄送锦旗，要求他及各级领导善待残疾人。后案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈庚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建省福州市平潭县法轮功学员，教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日早上，陈庚打算去学校给学生上课时，被围堵的警方抓捕，遭法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。陈庚据理上诉，却被驳回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，陈庚在被拘留<span lang="EN-US">275</span>天后，被劫入福清镜洋监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈光平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，江西省景德镇市中级人民法院退休法官，网名：亦忱。陈光平因在微博等多个平台发文质疑乐平警方办理的一宗经济案件存在警黑勾结栽赃嫁祸的情况，称江西景德镇乐平市公安局经侦大队副大队长邵长斌等人为“黑警”并向扫黑办进行了举报，结果被对方反诉诽谤并被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈光平是于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被一审判决犯诽谤罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，并被当场收监。陈光平已上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈国江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年出生，贵州省籍人，化名陈天河、熊焰，又被外卖骑手与工运支持者称为陈生，早期曾作街边摆摊个体户和工地搬运工，前北京市某饭店餐厅老板，全国著名外卖平台“美团”和“饿了么”北京市快递员，“外送江湖骑士联盟” 微信群组建者，北京外卖骑士联盟“盟主”，外卖联盟维权者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自幼出生于贵州省一个农村家庭，在父母频繁争吵中度过童年；五年级时，曾因家贫而辍学，随后靠在街边摆摊、在工地搬砖度日；后又辗转来到北京，自此成为一名北漂；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾受雇于一家餐厅专职送餐；后又开始制作网页版订餐网站，承包了附近所有网吧的订餐业务，并用积累下来的积蓄开办了一家小型餐馆；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，又开办另一家较大型饭店，但因长期经营亏损，随被迫转而成为送外卖小哥，亦因此事，其妻与其离婚，携幼子另嫁；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年起，曾因在送外卖工作中发现骑手们的生存环境十分恶劣，送餐服务的单价不断下降，无休息日，事故频发却得不到保障，无话语权，遂与骑手朋友组建“外送江湖骑士联盟”微信群，其为“盟主”；在此期间，曾因经常慷慨解囊协助失意投靠人度过难关，且致力于帮助骑手同行维权和鼓励彼此互助，故而深受众人好评和敬意；曾录制过百余条视频，向社会讲述外卖骑手们的遭遇和心酸，希望赢得支持和关注；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因外卖平台统一压低骑手送餐单价，为维护外卖骑手权益，其力挺发动骑手们拒绝接单，称前<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天不送“美团”，后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天不送“饿了么”，并让其各自打印通知，贴在外卖箱后边；然而传单尚未发出，其旋即被北京警方抓走，共计拘留<span lang="EN-US">26</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，北京外卖快递员为了生计和响应疫情防控就地过年，继续留京工作跑单，但因“饿了么”、“美团”等外卖平台刻意设置额外超级工作量，以使快递员因完不成任务而被克扣奖金，其为追诉公道，再次组织同行抵制外卖平台压榨骑手的劳工权益，但很快遭打压，与多名相关快递员被北京市朝阳区警方抓捕，罪由不清，至今不予释放；外界普遍疑称，因其组建的“外送江湖骑士联盟”群组，已联系有上万名骑手，影响力甚大，成为实质上的外卖骑手“工会”和维权组织，遂令中共当局感到恐惧，故而被抓。陈国江的家属于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日收到了其被正式逮捕的通知书。目前被羁押于北京市朝阳区看守所（北京市朝阳区朝阳北路<span lang="EN-US">29</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">100023</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东法轮功学员。广东雷州市白沙镇梛楠村人，后在湛江霞山区租住，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月末，在雷州市向民众发放法轮功资料的时候，被告，遭关押了几天后，获释，回到自己租住的房子。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初，陈海霞又被警察绑架、抄家。后遭判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在血压高不适合关押的情况下，中院维持冤判，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被关押到广州女子监狱迫害。目前，陈海霞被洗脑灌输、野蛮灌食，眼睛赤红、非常憔悴，仅一个月余，其境况令家人十分担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈洪伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，别名陈宏伟，辽宁省康平县人，康平县体校家属楼北栋<span lang="EN-US">5</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">501</span>号公民，辽宁伟业律师事务所律师，贪腐举报人，维权律师，中国在押维权人士。自成为执业律师并在辽宁伟业律师事务所任职以来，一直勤勉工作，认真执业；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾因康平县开发区管委会与开发区朝阳工业园内养殖小区的被拆迁户谈判陷入僵局，被该管委会聘请为法务工作代理，前去与被拆迁户协商拆迁事宜；为支持政府工作，其接受了此一聘请委托，并以先难后易等方式耐心做到与拆迁户的协商工作；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾先后三次从开发区财政局借款共计<span lang="EN-US">103</span>万元，且自搭<span lang="EN-US">1.46</span>万元，全部如数如约支付给被拆迁户作为补偿款，得到众被拆迁户的广泛认可；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因对当地政府的招标行为及相关部门官员的贪腐问题不满，声称要对县里的主要领导温某予以举报，随后不久立遭打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区警方以涉嫌“行贿罪”抓捕，后被留置；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被以涉嫌“贪污罪、行贿罪”转为刑拘，后知被疑指与十几年前其协助当地开发区拆迁和送某领导洗浴卡有关；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市和平区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并被关押于沈阳市和平区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区法院一审以“贪污罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；以“行贿罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；以“诈骗罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万元，数罪并罚决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元；其不服判决，立即上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，经沈阳市中级法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判；其坚称无罪，再次提起申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，经沈阳市中级法院再审，依然维持原判，驳回申诉；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。目前仍被羁押于沈阳市和平区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑尚不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陈开奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">41</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省莆田市人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被福建省宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，其与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨雄、庄友布、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，陈开奇被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈继海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住吉林市丰满区二道乡张家村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吉林市公安局及下属派出所警察抓捕至少有<span lang="EN-US">21</span>名法轮功学员、二名家属，法轮功学员陈继海、宋德满是其中两位。被关押一年余，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈继海和宋德满分别被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现在吉林省第二监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈家鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：又名陈文胆，字数真。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生于北流隆盛镇平坡村立新组。<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年容县师范毕业后在北流从教，后获北京科技进修学院律师函授班结业，中国逻辑与语言函授大学行政法专业毕业。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年分别在北流市、玉林市创办了老好人写作代理和金头脑文案写作代理服务部。后陈家鸿通过司法考试在广西百举鸣律师事务所执业，成为一名正式执业律师。源于陈家鸿长期参与维权敏感案件从而不断遭到当局的打压。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，陈家鸿律师介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，曾遭广西警持枪围困。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，广西律协官网发布了对陈家鸿律师的“公开谴责行业处分的通报”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，陈家鸿律师被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，广西南宁市司法局宣布解散百举鸣律师事务所，所有律师被要求转去其他律所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，陈家鸿律师被北流市公安局、玉林市公安局联合抓捕，家中也被抄了一些卷宗和其他东西。后获知被刑事拘留。后遭批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，陈家鸿涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权案”在广西玉林市中级人民法院开审。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">其一直坚称无罪，且因患有高血压及脑萎缩等病症，健康状况极差。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，玉林市中院宣判陈家鸿煽动颠覆国家政权罪成，判处有期徒刑三年。目前被羁押于广西玉林市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_81.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_81.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈建芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海著名维权人士、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“曹顺利人权捍卫者纪念奖”获奖人。陈建芳从一位抗争土地权的农民开始，长期从事维权活动。十多年前，她家的土地被上海市政府和房屋开发商非法征收和抢占，因得不到合法合理的安置补偿，走上了上访之路捍卫自己的权益。在多年的维权与打压的磨练中，陈建芳逐渐成为当地土地征收和房屋拆迁受害者的代言人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈建芳和曹顺利女士共同接受邀请，参加当月在日内瓦举办的人权培训活动并同时观摩联合国人权理事会会议。陈建芳在广州机场被阻拦出境。在同一天，曹顺利女士在北京机场被警方拦截并被强迫失踪。警方将陈建芳带回上海并对其拘留、调查讯问、并密切监视多日。陈建芳的人权倡导活动，招来当局对她不断地打击报复，包括恐吓，殴打和任意拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早晨八点陈建芳在家中遭上海警方秘密抓捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，被上海市浦东新区检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”批捕，被指控因为聚集举牌、拉横幅、网络言论等违法了国家法律。后遭起诉。遭中共当局司法机关的违法阻扰，律师一直无法介入案件。目前陈建芳女士被羁押于上海市看守所。当局始终不准其代理律师会见。后于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日获悉，陈建芳被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">成都青白江区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁。在原川化集团公司青上公司上班。在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年迫害法轮功后，陈洁多次被青白江区法院判刑，第一次于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，第二次于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早上，陈洁将一本《共产主义的终极目的》发到了青白江区大弯派出所的警察手中，被该警察抓捕，在对陈洁作出十天治安拘留后，在陈洁被关押的第八天，治安拘留改为刑事拘留。第<span lang="EN-US">12</span>天左右，构陷她的案件被移送到青白江区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人毕业于清华大学法学院，中国资深的媒体人，先后在《南方周末》、《中国青年报》、《新京报》、《人民日报》等媒体上发表了<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多篇评论文章。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年以中国青年报记者身份踢爆武汉女大学生卖淫现象，造成轰动，但却被解雇；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年作为公益时报主编，签发批评文章，触怒当局再被炒；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月因“批评政府过多”遭人民日报解除人民网江苏视窗执行总编职务。陈杰人多年来发表数千文章，希望推进新闻自由，并倡导以网络为平台的草根监督和公民表达。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，陈杰人曾在网上公开实名举报湖南邵阳市纪委书记邓广雁严重失职和渎职。随后几天，陈杰人就下落不明，与外界失联。有消息透露，湖南公安以“涉嫌敲诈勒索、非法经营”等罪名“依法办理”陈杰人。目前，陈杰人的微信公众号显示“由用户投诉并经平台审核，涉嫌违反相关法律法规，账号已被停止使用”。后获知遭湖南警方刑事拘留。湖南省桂阳县人民法院网站发布消息：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午，湖南省桂阳县人民法院公开开庭，对被告人陈杰人、陈伟人、刘敏寻衅滋事、敲诈勒索、非法经营、行贿一案宣告一审判决，对被告人陈杰人以寻衅滋事罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法经营罪、行贿罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">701</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈景捷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江安达市女法轮功学员。原安达市糖厂职工，。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日晚赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被警察等非法闯入各自的家中抓捕的。赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷被关押在安达看守所。后获悉裴玉凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，陈景捷被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。赵秀芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，以有人举报为由，德惠市天台乡派出所和德惠国保联合绑架陈娟，并拘留十天，后陈娟被取保回家。迫害期间，因陈娟是做熟食生意，店铺生计需要她，家人着急营救，被德惠国保勒索五万元取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，德惠市六一零公安局国保大队将陈娟拉到德惠市民心医院检查身体，后又把她带到长春医院检查身体。当天陈娟被放回家中，并被告知称，关于她的所谓材料已递交到德惠市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被德惠市法院非法开庭，历时四十多分钟。当时没有宣判，称让陈娟回家等结果。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，吉林省长春德惠市法轮功学员陈娟被关押到长春“病监大队”。清明街与北安路交汇的长春市医院公安局设立的所谓“病监大队”，对外挂的牌子是口腔门诊，实质是迫害法轮功学员的黑窝，很多老年法轮功学员非法被关在这里遭迫害。现获悉，长春市德惠市法轮功学员陈娟已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，仍被关押在“病监大队”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html#2213222346-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html#2213222346-2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈立红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：沈阳市铁西区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午四点左右，在沈阳市铁西区启工二校门口，陈立红将两份《给善良人的一封信》真相传单送给了停在校门前的大客车上两个当兵的小伙手上，那两个小伙还乐呵呵的接过来。陈立红继续往前走，走了十来米，那两个当兵的赶上来把陈立红围住，打了报警电话。随后陈立红被绑架到沈阳市铁西区分局七路派出所。陈立红被关押在沈阳市第一看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被沈阳市铁西区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>“中国审判流程信息公开网”通知案子已结案，陈立红被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈丽萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁沈阳市法轮功学员。原沈阳市辽中县（现辽中区）六间房学校优秀教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，陈敏在豪林购物中心门口给人讲法轮功遭迫害真相时，遭一便衣抓捕抄家。后被辽中区法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">陈强：</b>河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后陈强被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈三灵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省界首市王集镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而被多次遭界首市公安局及王集镇派出所骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月又因宣传法轮功资料而被非法拘捕，自此失联，近期得知他已被界首市检察院批捕。现被关押在安徽省阜阳市看守所。后案件音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈少天：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，曾用名陈志伟，河南省周口市扶沟县古城乡尧岗村人，原为农民，后成为某公司一名大货车司机，网络活跃人士，网名“天哥（<span lang="EN-US">@tiange88</span>）”，网红，人称河南“国骂哥”，社会正义人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，曾因是一名大货车司机，在武汉病毒疫情肆意蔓延之时，遇政府封城且全国各地农村纷纷挖沟挡板、禁止行人及车辆通行，随发“国骂”视频而不料迅速在网上走红；曾因以智慧方式骂警察但又只字不提警察，骂政府官员却又从不指名道姓，比如他曾暗喻：“第一产业养牛养羊，第二产业杀牛宰羊，第三产业吃牛肉喝羊汤，第四产业，文化产业———吹牛<span lang="EN-US">X</span>，出洋相”，凡此种种，因其国骂内容引发社会热议和网友关注，随被有心网民将其头像制成漫画、微信表情包，在朋友圈内疯传，又被网友堪称“国骂哥”；然而，基于其视频传速太快，在引发网民关注的同时，亦被中国网信和公安系统即刻关注、警觉，并迅速在敌情通报上记下其名；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因公开武汉病毒疫情的“吹哨人”李文亮医生因感染疫病去世，其再次在社交媒体上国骂，故而其微信、抖音、快手尽被禁言，最终促其从微信平台转向国际媒体平台<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>继续国骂发声；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被扶沟县警方传唤带走，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被扶沟县警方执行逮捕；后很快又被扶沟县检察院以同罪名提起公诉，指控其在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月期间，利用<span lang="EN-US">3</span>部苹果手机自拍视频并在推特上发布，其中<span lang="EN-US">50</span>条是“炒作中国国内的热敏感事件，攻击政治体制，侮辱丑化国家工作人员”视频，因其言行“严重损坏了国家形象，危害了国家利益，破坏了社会秩序”，已构成了寻衅滋事罪，但因其系初犯，认罪认罚，遂建议法院在量刑上可从轻处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在河南省扶沟县法院正式开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被扶沟县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；目前被羁押于扶沟县看守所（河南省周口市扶沟县柴岗乡张力士村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">461300</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈世贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川成都市金牛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵正在友人毛坤家做客休息，被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，毛坤、杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑，陈世贵判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陈树庆</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，浙江省富阳县人，自由撰稿人，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中国民主党全国筹委会负责人之一，人权活动家，<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学生。<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因其多次参与民主活动，并参与联署呼吁释放包括异议人士吕耿松在内的大陆被拘捕人士，随遭到当局报复性打压，并被警方两次以“颠覆国家政权”罪由传唤；至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，终被杭州市警方以“颠覆国家政权罪”正式刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被杭州市检察院正式批捕。目前被羁押于浙江省杭州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日在杭州中院开庭，未判决。经延期与退侦后，此案于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午宣判，陈树庆被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏固原市隆德县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，大专文化，内科主治医师，系原隆德县医院医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午，陈淑琴给路人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>份法轮功资料让他去了解，不料被此人恶告，随后被城关派出所两个警察抓捕。隆德国保大队王胜强带人抄家及到单位搜查，抢走所有大法书籍，笔记本计算机等部份私人物品。陈淑琴当时被王胜强等人抓捕到固原市看守所，看守所拒收。国保人员给陈淑琴办了取保候审。陈淑琴回家并正常上班，大约在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬突然失踪。后获悉，陈淑琴又被抓捕、批捕。陈淑琴被关押在宁夏固原市看守所。后获悉，陈淑琴医生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被关押到宁夏女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈书义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省涞水县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。河北省涞水县王村镇东王庄村人。一九九九年七月，中共发动对法轮功的残酷迫害后，老人曾两次被劳教：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，时年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的法轮功学员陈书义被警察入室抓捕。次日下午两点，陈书义被刑事拘留，被关押到涞水看守所至今。后获悉涿州市法院对陈书义秘密庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。而他家人既没接到开庭通知，也没接到判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈爽：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市温泉居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在深圳市龙岗区打工期间被深圳龙岗区警方非法以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘。目前被关押在深圳市龙岗区看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">约于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被深圳市龙岗区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈松艳</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。她孝敬老人、家庭和睦，是遵守法律、遵守社会公德的好市民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，陈松艳在北安市金街附近向民众讲述法轮功真相，遭不明真相的人构陷，被警察绑架。她先后被劫持到五大连池拘留所、黑河市看守所关押迫害。后遭逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，北安市法院在黑河市爱辉区法院对陈松艳第一次庭审。非法庭审结束时，没有宣判。后来家属被告知，陈松艳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。陈松艳上诉到中级法院。被驳回。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈天茂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建晋江维权人士。现关押在福建晋江看守所。陈案缘起于其担任合同制警察期间，在一次执行公务发生车祸而致的工伤。因工伤引发被辞退，住房被分给他人，以及待遇等纠纷，多年来陈为维权，进行了多次诉讼，多次上访，多次被拘留，又被劳教，差点被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年底前因涉嫌为境外提供国家秘密罪被逮捕，他坚定地认为自己无罪。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈武权：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东维权律师陈武权因守护家乡海滩被以涉寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，同时被刑事拘留的还有其同村村民<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人。陈武权是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日下午，应当地信访部门的通知，与<span lang="EN-US">6</span>位村民一起去谈话，但他们<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人随后被以阻挠开工的名义抓走。其中<span lang="EN-US">1</span>位村民之后被放出来，其余<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被湛江市经济技术开发区公安分局刑事拘留。之前，当地官方试图在陈武权家乡所在的海域填海，而他带领家乡的村民，捍卫他们世代赖以维生的海洋。根据村民所发布的图片和申诉材料显示，随着官方开始围堰填海，原本海产丰富的海滩和红树林都遭到严重破坏，世代渔民赖以维生的螺、蚝、沙虫等海产已经消失。村民被迫出来护海。在去年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，村民的现场护海行动受到当地警方镇压。而陈武权发布的相关文件还显示，他们已经多次向有关部门反映，希望能够叫停填海工程，但官方的回复否认填海破坏环境，并认为渔民要转型谋出路在多方申诉无门之后，陈武权日前在网上发布要求游行示威的申请，很多村民已签名。陈武权之前曾代理多宗维权案，其中最为人关注的是陈光诚侄儿陈克贵案，因此多次受官方打压，并被吊销执业资格。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，广东湛江市经济技术开发区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处陈武权有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。同时被抓捕的村民陈伟梁、陈振明、陈还森、陈春霖、陈帅、陈隆群等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半有期徒刑。陈武权自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。广东人权律师陈武权于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日转往广东四会监狱（位于广东肇庆市）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈晓彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈晓梅：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，家住黑龙江省伊春市伊春区。陈晓梅因<span lang="EN-US">30</span>年未判决的案子上北京上访多次。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被伊春市公安局以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日移送伊春市法院起诉，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日退侦，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日重新起诉，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>号上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，伊春市上甘岭区法院将以敲诈勒索罪开审陈晓梅。伊春市上甘岭区检察院称：陈晓梅采取到北京非正常上访，要挟负有稳控责任单位负责人，索要公私财物，数额较大，应当以敲诈勒索罪追求其刑事责任。目前案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;
