mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈新年：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南南阳唐河县油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日陈新年、彭涛夫妇在南阳油田采油二厂，讲法轮功时，被不明真相的人诬告，被唐河县滨河派出所警察抓捕，被抄家，陈新年被关押在唐河县看守所。后家属被告知其已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，关押到郑州监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈星伯</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河北省邢台市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，曾任河北省邢台市广播电台主任编辑、专题部副主任。因修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被邢台市公安局信都区分局国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，邢台市襄都区法院对陈星伯判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。陈星伯本人提出上诉，被邢台市中级法院无理驳回，并维持非法原判。两次开庭均秘密进行。非法判决书下达后，陈星伯的单位将他双开，即开除公职、开除党籍，已停发养老金及一切待遇。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，陈星伯已被监禁在河北省冀东分局第四监狱（河北唐山监狱），至今没有任何消息。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秀洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁锦州市北镇市沟帮子镇王屯村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，陈秀洁因在家中和另外二人一起读书，被沟帮子派出所警察抓捕并被抄家，之后办理了取保后回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，陈秀洁在家中被沟帮子镇派出所警察再次抓捕，并被送到锦州女子看守所，后经凌海市法院构陷判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，陈秀洁从锦州女子看守所被送到辽宁省女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秀萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈雪清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，广东省韶关市曲江区法轮功学员。一九六二年十月出生，大专毕业，韶关钢铁集团公司退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年因讲真相陈雪清被曲江区法院判刑三年。陈雪清<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年才出冤狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，陈雪清发现曲江区松山街道韶钢红旗区居委会有诋毁、诬陷法轮功的宣传栏，就用油漆将这个宣传栏销毁，被居委会诬告。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，陈雪清被曲江区公安分局抓捕。后得知，陈雪清已被曲江区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈岩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁抚顺法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年曾遭受三年冤狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日才释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈艳群</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：原是陕西省城固县龙头镇卫生院职工，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因举报卫生院院长的贪污腐败行为遭到打击报复，其劳动报酬被克扣，造成高职低薪的尴尬局面。之后，陈艳群找到院长办公室，要求公开卫生院的财务收支明细，做到同工同酬，被院长夫妻打成重伤。陈艳群住院治疗期间受到人为干扰，耽误了最佳治疗时机，后经鉴定为六级伤残，留下了严重的后遗症。陈艳群伤情好转后开始上访，要求依法追究打人者的刑事责任及其贪污公款的法律责任，结果遭到劫访人员多次殴打、非法拘禁、拘留的处罚。维权近十多年，陈艳群曾参与公民围观活动，声援秦永敏；围观张扣扣案件的庭审；在县政府门口举牌。陈艳群是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午到城固县一宾馆寻找工作组反映问题时被城固县公安局拦截带回，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被城固县公安局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，后批捕、起诉。。其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪一案，陕西城固县法院于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9:00</span>开庭。陈艳群被检察院建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">4-5</span>年。现羁押在汉中市汉台看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈跃飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市武清区河西务镇法轮功学员。女，家住天津市武清区河西务镇东西陈庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分左右，陈跃飞被闯入家中的河西务派出所警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被非法庭审。目前得知，陈跃飞女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈鹰军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西咸阳网民陈鹰军、王兴杰等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>人因在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传播涉及政治的内容于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被咸阳市秦都区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半有期徒刑。判决书指控他们通过<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群有组织地传播“涉及政治的谣言”，攻击政府、党和国家领导人。被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名陕西咸阳网民分别是：陈鹰军、王兴杰、卢向辉、刘芗、周昱、朱远亮、李好轩、徐海波、李泰营、周福评、潘建、廖焕华、武刚。其中，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陈鹰军在庭审中只高喊口号，不做辩护，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期最重。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈友荣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁，内燃机车厂子弟校教师，多次被抓捕迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被抓捕到楠木寺女子劳教所迫害一年半，在被非法劳教期间，遭残酷迫害、毒刑拷打。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">4</span>点～<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点钟，资阳市雁江区「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」与国保大队<span lang="EN-US">7</span>至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个公安以查户口为借口，闯入陈友荣家抄家，并强行抓捕陈友荣到二娥湖洗脑班迫害。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个多月后又被逮捕，之后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈昱昊：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，广东省汕头市人，网名“宫本美代子”，“萌娘百科”巡查员，音<span lang="EN-US">MAD</span>作者与<span lang="EN-US">BB</span>剧场（即以<span lang="EN-US">BB/GB</span>素材等制作的动画）作者，恶俗维基管理员，哲学中文维基行政员，人称“陈导师”，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于南方医科大学，并在南方医院进行实习；大学毕业后，因转行在“萌娘百科”上当巡查员，曾上传过大量含恶俗维基内容的相关文件，并积极撰写页面，故为恶俗维基的美化宣传立下了汗马功劳。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在<span lang="EN-US">B</span>站（即<span lang="EN-US">bilibili</span>（<span lang="EN-US">NASDAQ</span>：<span lang="EN-US">BILI</span>），全称为“哔哩哔哩弹幕网”的简称，创立于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，现为中国大陆境内最大的年轻人潮流文化娱乐小区）的音乐区发布过“迫真东方”同人的音乐，即纪念某次学运歌曲的倒放混响版本，故有较高人气度。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾因中文曲奇（即大部分东方合同常用的动画企画视频及由此产生的网络模因的概称）维基和中文银梦（即中文与互联网界相契合的淫梦百科全书及相应文化简称）维基陆续建立，随经商议后暂返恶俗维基作编辑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因“恶俗维基”与多家恶俗圈网热发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的相关讯息（含户籍、照片等个人信息），遂立遭当局严厉打压。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部成立项目组，开始对全国各恶俗网站会员实施统一大抓捕，但后经严格审讯，发觉其成员大多年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，遂准予各地警方纷纷放人，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功嘉奖，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，且上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把其所辖维基成员全部抓捕。在当时，其虽并非两个网站的核心人物，亦未参与过“支纳维基”挂网披露习近平等国家领导人亲属讯息的活动，但仍于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被广东省茂名市警方予以抓捕，后被暂短指定居所监视居住和刑拘。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，涉案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，其被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。其等均表不服，已提起上诉，二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈玉花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、山东菏泽市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十多岁，菏泽市牡丹区商业系统退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程盼云、李振环、陈玉花三位法轮功女学员开着电轿车下乡，在当地农村散发法轮功真相资料，在菏泽市牡丹区安兴镇被牡丹区公安局国保大队警察跟踪抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈云飞：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，四川省达州市达县人，个体农场主和农艺师，民主“业余驯兽师”，四川“民主行为艺术家”，著名维权公民、异议人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年曾参与过“<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运”，六四镇压后返乡谋生，仍坚守民主理念，在当地展开多种帮助访民的维权活动，后因多次试图前往北京祭奠前中共总书记赵紫阳而被成都警方长期监控、威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在《成都晚报》刊登“向坚强的六四遇难者母亲致敬”的广告，被成都警方抓捕，后被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”监视居住半年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因以发起人名义与维权公民谭作人、冉云飞等捐血纪念六四而被警方警告、威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因被怀疑参与“茉莉花革命”而被警方软禁家中多日；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因不满和抗议当局禁止其出境旅行，而为其护照和港澳通行证举行别样葬礼，自此开中国此类葬礼之先河；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因向四川省人大常委会递交“致习近平等先生的公开信”、“要求中国最有权力的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名部级以上官员公开财产的公民建议书”以及<span lang="EN-US">7033</span>名有效公民的签名名单，而被拒绝签收；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因租赁房屋被当局联合黑社会逼迁，搬迁中又遭遇暴徒的殴打和恶警的威胁攻击，终致其身体严重受损；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，又因其开通“成都市区到彭州中石化厂一日游旅游线路”而被当局忌恨，其活动随即被成都市警方搅局破坏。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其与维权公民<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余人到成都市新津县为当年的六四死难学生肖杰、吴国峰扫墓，遂在返程途中遭到上百名持枪特警的围追堵截，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日即被四川省新津县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪名正式批捕。后检察院取消“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”，只以寻衅滋事罪起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日陈云飞被成都武侯区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日刑满释放。陈云飞于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>号晚上被</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">警察带走。<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日警察到他家里，将他的母亲送到了成都市温江区的侄儿家中。后获悉陈云飞被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，北京张磊律师在成都市陴都区看守所会见了陈云飞。陈云飞<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被从陴都区的住处抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被以寻衅滋事罪名执行逮捕。陈云飞非常乐观，表示在看守所里一切都好，就像是换了一个地方工作，在哪里都可以帮助他人，都可以传福音，被关在看守所里的人更需要他传福音。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈云飞寻衅滋事案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日移送成都市陴都区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，陈云飞昨被当局构陷获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。中共法院官方通告如下：“<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，四川省成都市郫都区人民法院对被告人陈云飞强制猥亵、猥亵儿童一案依法不公开审理，并公开宣判，以被告人陈云飞犯强制猥亵罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；犯猥亵儿童罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；数罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。”刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/4.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/4.html</span></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈泽奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，山西省太原市杏花岭区人，广东省深圳市龙岗区居民，深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部经理，计算机软件专家，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。在深圳从业<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，曾任职于多家公司的软件部负责人，为人谦和儒雅，工作成绩卓越，尤其是在深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部担任经理时，曾参与过多项软件开发，且主持研发的掌上电脑“一指禅”及“蓝精灵数码词典”是当时优秀的高新技术产品；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，而遭中共深圳当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，突然被深圳市龙岗区警方从家中抓捕刑拘，并被送往深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，指控其“系法轮功组织成员”，利用掌握的专业技术，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功，属违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案在深圳市龙岗区法院正式庭审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后经深圳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈兆志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京科技大学退休教师。陈兆志<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生人，身患多种疾病，高血压，脑梗等。陈兆志被刑事拘留的时间应该在疫情期间，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日以后。其<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>账号最后更新时间是<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，最后的两条推分别是：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2/13/2020 </span>路安艾时评：中共官场大斗争，习派人马全面接管王派系体现中共内部什么信号？气化炉到底意味着什么？<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、武汉肺炎风声鹤唳！ 习近平下死令 「应收尽收」储备<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万张床位背后。陈兆志遭抓捕的具体原因目前还不清楚。去年<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午在八宝山革命公墓门前，当领导的车队来临时，北京科技大学教授陈兆志举拳高呼：打倒李鹏！李鹏是刽子手！当场被警察抓走，遭殴打，后获释。陈兆志已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被海淀区检察院批准逮捕，其涉嫌罪名由刑事拘留时的“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”变更为“寻衅滋事罪”。委托律师<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬前往海淀区看守所会见了陈兆志。陈兆志的疫情言论包括“武汉病毒不是中国病毒，是中共病毒”等，他认为这是中共在对他进行政治迫害和侵害言论自由，因此拒绝在审讯笔录上签字。已被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，北京科技大学退休教师陈兆志寻衅滋事案正在北京海淀法院山后法庭开庭审理。中午，陈兆志老师庭审结束，公诉机关建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，当庭未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程德亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东烟台法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，程德亮和妻子唐玉兰同时从家中被烟台开发区金桥派出所警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被关进看守所，其中，程德亮被关在烟台开发区（第二）看守所，唐玉兰被关在烟台市看守所（位于福山东留公村南）。唐玉兰于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日回家，程德亮一直被非法关押在第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，检察院将此案交到开发区法院。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午两点半，在开发区法院，程德亮被非法开庭，他的律师做了无罪释放的辩护，当庭没公布结果。在被关押<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月后，程德亮遭烟台开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程桂靖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，天津市南开区法轮功学员，因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖姐妹被天津警方抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖被检察院批捕。随后由南开分局预审科张伟以两人用手机打电话诉说法轮功学员被迫害事实真相为由，先后三次把构陷她们的材料上报南开检察院起诉，其中两次因证据不足退回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南开法院判以重刑，并勒索高额罚金：<a name="_Hlk52179872">程桂英被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；</a>程桂靖被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。程桂英、程桂靖对判决提出上诉。天津第二中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。家属被索要高额罚款。关押在南开看守所。刑期至：<a name="_Hlk52179802"><span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52179802;"></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2020/9/22/%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%A7%90%E5%A6%B9%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-412109.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52179802;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52179802;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程桂英：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52179802;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，天津市南开区法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖姐妹被天津警方抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖被检察院批捕。随后由南开分局预审科张伟以两人用手机打电话诉说法轮功学员被迫害事实真相为由，先后三次把构陷她们的材料上报南开检察院起诉，其中两次因证据不足退回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南开法院判以重刑，并勒索高额罚金：程桂英被诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；程桂靖被诬判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。程桂英、程桂靖对判决提出上诉。天津第二中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。家属被索要高额罚款。关押在南开看守所。刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2020/9/22/%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%A7%90%E5%A6%B9%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-412109.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">程进峰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：陕西省榆林市“三赎基督”信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被执行逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被宁夏回族自治区石嘴山市中级法院二审维持一审，以组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程全云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京通州法轮功学员。程全云<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被抓捕抄家，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被批捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。信息来源<span lang="EN-US">:<o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/11/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432426.html#211010222223-2"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/11/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432426.html#211010222223-2</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程西江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">济南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日当天，济南市铁路派出所再次抓捕法轮功学员尹峰，警察同时对最近曾与尹峰有过交往的、居住在朝阳小区的法轮功学员程西江陈连美等法轮功学员抄家、抓捕。程西江被抄走打印机、电脑、大法书籍和一些《九评》、《共产主义的终极目的》等物品和书籍。当日下午，尹峰被逼交<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金后回家。程西江、陈连美被关押在济南铁路看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被秘密审判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程学珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。程学珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程渊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，广东省深圳市常驻居民，中国民间公益机构“长沙富能”创办人（之一）、工作人员，乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者等群体维权诉讼代理人，中国在押政治犯。因从事公益维权活动<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余年，曾代理过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多起乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者维权诉讼案，颇受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾首例成功代理江西省进贤县艾滋就业歧视案，为当事人争得赔偿，经多家媒体报导而广为人知，但亦引起中共当局的高度警觉及跟踪监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，突然被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从深圳跨境带走，并被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；审讯期间，被多次问及其在长沙富能所做的工作内容、资金来源及其近期外出活动（含去香港，与香港记者录像等）都做些什么等细节详情；据悉，被抓当天，其家属多受牵连，其妻竟被戴黑头套遭无辜审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">17</span>小时，其<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁半幼女遭惊吓，夜晚睡觉出现抽搐和梦呓，白天表现惊恐异常，其兄程浩、其老父亲等均遭警告恐吓；其代理律师欲了解案件详情遭绝，仅告知其罪名及法定的拘留期限；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭起诉，并被遭强行委派官派律师，对家属严密封锁，拒不见面。家属外界都无法获知案情进展。已经开庭审理，家属仍然对信息一无所知。被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：长沙富能公益案之程渊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑，现在于湖南赤山监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程志春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省四平市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年生。程志春曾曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，程志春被四平市铁西区仁兴派出所抄家、抓捕，由于疫情暂放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日左右，程志春被公安方面下书告知，被四平铁西检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日后执行。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在吉林省女子监狱遭受迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%9C%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B3%E5%B8%8278%E5%B2%81%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E7%A8%8B%E5%BF%97%E6%98%A5%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-430476.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/6/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E7%9C%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B3%E5%B8%8278%E5%B2%81%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E7%A8%8B%E5%BF%97%E6%98%A5%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-430476.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次成加材（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，又名次成坚参，笔名“秀真”，前四川甘孜州白玉佛学院僧人，前西北民族大学中文文学专业学生，西藏知名青年藏汉双语作家，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年进入四川甘孜州白玉佛学院为僧，学习藏传佛教知识，截止<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾先后在色达五明佛学院及德格协庆寺等多个寺庙进行过深造，并在此期间勤耕不缀，于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年出版发行《雪域悲歌》、《雪域命运》等多部藏文著作；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年底还俗进入西北民族大学攻读中文文学写作专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年在该大学与其他同学联合创办了《新一代》藏文杂志，担任主编，同时，他还在藏人文化网开设的“秀真博客”里，用中文撰写过多篇文章，其中著名的有《丑陋的拉萨》、《那一夜》、《那些年、那些事》等等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因其多次在大学里举办各种被政府视为非法主题的讨论会，触及了当局的敏感神经，随被当局开除学籍，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月返乡后又开办了一所业余学校，向家乡青年进行免费藏汉双语教学。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，由于比如县比如乡莫阿村、孟庆村和达塘乡等地发生多处藏人示威行动，以抗议当局强行开展“爱国再教育、家家挂红旗”的政治宣讲活动，故而被警方指控在县学校学生集体抗议和民众绝食示威等事件中有“煽动分裂国家”、“破坏社会稳定”、“公开发表非法言论”之嫌，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被警方拘捕并抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被西藏自治区高级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”和“破坏社会稳定罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">次成嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州夏河县九甲乡人，夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。自幼即进入拉卜楞寺为僧；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因对中共当局高压严管制度的不满，甘肃省甘南州夏河县发生了大规模僧俗藏人的抗议游行，其亦参与其中；又因被当局视为带头抗议者，随在当局对抗议藏民展开大逮捕后被迫逃离；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被甘南州警方在舟曲县抓捕刑拘，并送至甘肃省安全厅看守所关押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其不服上诉，后经甘南州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；</b>据悉，其在关押期间，曾惨遭刑讯逼供；从被捕至判刑以来，其私聘律师权、亲属探视权及到法庭旁听审判权均被拒绝；因其行为仅为以和平抗议方式来表达内心诉求，却遭司法枉法重判，故而随后又在夏河县城、拉卜楞寺院内外出现大量抗议传单。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，次成嘉措获减刑，刑期减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。次成嘉措<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月经甘肃省天水市中级人民法院批准，被予以减刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。这是他获得第二次减刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次旺（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">西藏索县赤多乡人，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，索县赤多乡珍达寺僧人，藏族良心犯。因关注西藏问题，被中共当局长期秘密监控，并被警方几次拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被当地警方第一次刑捕，非法关押半年后取保候审释放。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日第二次又被刑拘，当时和他一同遭捕的还有珍达寺诵经师仓央嘉措、僧人阿次和坚参。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年初左右，被中共西藏当局强行指控非法，以不知由罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次旺嘉措：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tsewang Gyatso</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，中国在押政治犯。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾， 随于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">仓央嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区那曲人，藏族僧人，那曲地区索县赤多乡珍达寺（又称直达寺）诵经师、财务主管，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共当局发现西藏那曲地区索县有人利用手机和微信传播所谓 “禁止材料”（如转发印有达赖喇嘛的图片、传播涉及民族尊严的歌曲及透露被封锁的地方消息等），且在围墙上喷涂“西藏独立”等字样，遂展开大规模抓捕行动；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，多名当地僧侣及村民被当局以莫须有罪名拘捕，多数人长期下落不明，仓央嘉措亦于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被当地警方从寺庙驻地抓走，后以涉嫌“与境外联系”及“煽动他人反政府”罪由刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被当局以“向外界保持联络”和“鼓励该寺年轻僧人反抗中国政府活动”等罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被羁押于西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赤列（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，藏族，中国在押政治犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（注：当日是中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平抗议示威活动；但该活动立即惨遭当地警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使上百藏人被抓，多人被打死打伤；截止同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，共有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；其本人亦因积极参与抗议示威游行，很快被警方以“参与抗议示威活动”为由抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“在示威活动中实施打砸和抢夺财物”为罪由判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丛霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，丛霞外出贴法轮功材料，被大连西岗区国保大队和西岗区八一路派出所抓捕。后丛霞被构陷到大连西岗区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上诉，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二审被维持冤判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆维权人士。崔斌早在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因见义勇为，帮助消防武警官兵救人时，膝盖被武警踩伤，从而造成二级伤残。但重庆市政府不仅不依法承认他的见义勇为行为，更不按照相关法律政策给予奖励和救助，在万般无奈之下，他被迫走上了上访之路。期间，多次遭到重庆维稳部门删帖封号、监视居住、非法拘禁、拘留、殴打等一系列迫害。由此，崔斌由一位访民，逐渐成长为一名民主维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年因在北京二中院围观浦志强案而被抓进久敬庄，被关押五天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年参与声援郭飞雄签名活动，并在高笋塘步行街广场公开绝食以示声援，再遭传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月两会期间，崔斌因在北京拦截两会代表车辆，在重庆驻京办被关了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天黑监狱。之后被地方警察押送回家，再遭万州警方<span lang="EN-US">"</span>监视居住<span lang="EN-US">"</span>软禁一年。期间因外出没有事前“报告”，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。当地维稳部门一直是崔斌为“眼中钉肉中刺”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日崔斌就曾遭受过一次黑社会人员的殴打，那次是因为他进京上访，被重庆维稳部门所忌恨，于是他们指使黑社会人员用杀猪刀砍断了他双手的八根筋健和三根手指骨，并且全身多处被暴打砍伤。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，崔斌背着写有“孙政才独裁暴政腐化之风还在重庆漫延，重庆人民生活在水生火热之中”的牌子在高笋塘步行街广场游行，之后又穿着印有“当人民恐惧政府即为暴政”文化衫拍照并在网上传播，又遭传唤抄家。崔斌的处境日益艰难。长期以来，崔斌一直在当地警方的严密监控中，并被以各种方式，限制或变相限制其人身自由，尤其外出受到更明显的限制。崔斌自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日突然失联，后获悉：崔斌为自卫杀了维稳警察派去迫害他的黑帮人员，后遭刑事拘留。先是关押在重庆万州看守所。后获悉崔斌遭到起诉判刑，一直关押在重庆万州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，重庆维权公民前往万州看守所给崔斌上账<span lang="EN-US">,</span>遭到拒绝，后经询问得知崔斌已被判死缓，已由重庆万州看守所转到重庆蜀都监狱关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">崔德（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">又名崔成，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县查理乡夺哇村人，原查理寺僧人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔兰琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省任丘市吕公堡乡法轮功学员，吕公堡乡辛安庄村人。崔兰琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在北村讲真相，告诉人们瘟疫中如何自救，被吕公堡派出所巡警绑架。崔兰琴被关押在看守所，据悉于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日开庭。崔兰琴女儿在过年前给辩护律师打电话得知，她的妈妈被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔永强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日凌晨五点钟左右，崔永强在租住的地下室准备出门时，被蹲坑的四名便衣警察绑架。警察对他的住所进行了搜查。便衣警察没有出示搜查证，也没有出具扣押物品清单。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，崔永强被青岛市黄岛区法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">D.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">达吾提汗•达尔古色孜（哈萨克）、达日（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">代方盛<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丹增曲卡（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓成开、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜贺先、</span><span style="font-family: New Roman&quot;;">、段宜法、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）、多杰扎才（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达吾提汗﹒达尔古色孜（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县人，哈萨克族，博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县牧民，人权捍卫者。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县先后有<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多哈萨克族人（不分年龄、职业，甚至有年轻学生及政府公务员等）因“在微信群里，讨论如何移民哈萨克斯坦国”事宜被中共当局抓捕，其亦因关注移民事宜，并积极协助哈萨克村民移民哈萨克斯坦而在此次当局大抓捕中遭受迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月突然被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全罪”传唤、刑拘，后很快被温泉县检察院正式批捕，被指“帮人移民到哈萨克斯坦”就是犯了严重的政治问题。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县法院一审以“危害国家安全罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。其不服，已提起上诉。据悉，羁押期间曾惨遭酷刑毒打，病危住院，但出院后仍被立即重判，其要求聘请辩护律师也被拒绝。目前被羁押于新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与赞查（藏）二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">代方盛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">山东省青岛市法轮功学员。代方盛在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日中午，在青岛市南区延吉路发放法轮功资料，被人举报，并被中山路派出所抓捕后，被关押在即墨普东看守所。后代方盛被判刑</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年半。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日送济南监狱。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">丹增曲卡（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区拉萨市人，又名丹曲，藏名<span lang="EN-US"> Tenzin Choedak</span>或<span lang="EN-US">Tenchoe</span>，社会工作者，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代在印度达兰萨拉的西藏儿童村完成<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年级的教育课程；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年返回西藏，在当地的欧洲非政府组织红十字会工作，并在拉萨和日喀则等多个地区推动环保工作；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因参与拉萨的和平抗议活动，被当地警方拘捕。据悉，在拘捕期间曾遭遇严刑逼供，理由是其父曾在西藏政治舞台上活跃多年，但<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年被迫离开西藏流亡印度，严刑拷打他目的是确定其抗议行动是否受到父亲的影响；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚款人民币一万元，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓成开：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">绵阳市三台县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，绵阳市法轮功学员柳涛与三台县法轮功学员邓成开到三台县芦溪镇去买东西被抓捕。柳涛被关押在绵阳市看守所，邓成开被关押在三台县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，柳涛、邓承开被绵阳市三台县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金二千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓光英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆访民，被强制关押精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">23</span>点邓光英在北京市丰台区吕村被朱家坟派出所抓捕至今，邓光英的家人至今没有收到任何拘押通知。邓光英父亲还透露，地方政府的官员曾多次上门，要求在邓光英属于精神病人的材料上签字。对地方政府的无理要求，邓光英的父亲予以断然拒绝。一个没有任何精神病症状的正常人，只不过因为信访反映问题与争取自身权益，表达诉求，就属于精神病人，就要拘禁于精神病院，这就是社会主义官僚的固有思维，然而用践踏国家法律与公民人权的方式。至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月仍被精神病，未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邓桂英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">南昌市的法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。原为南昌市东风印刷厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年中秋节后，约<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，邓桂英与母亲在家中吃饭，被家中近亲打电话给国保，随后，邓桂英被南昌市青云谱国保大队、三店派出所警察抓捕。后邓桂英被关押在新建县南昌市第一看守所内。邓桂英被非法关押后，朋友们一直没有邓桂英的消息。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月才得到确切消息，邓桂英已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，但是目前，邓桂英被非法关押地点不详。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓国行</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河南商水县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，河南商水县姚集乡白茬村人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬去街上买馍时跟民众讲法轮功，遭人恶告，被警察抓捕到商水拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后被劫持到商水看守所关押。当时邓国行拒绝所谓“转化”，警察说：不转化永远不让出去。邓国行绝食反迫害，要求无条件放人。警察又利用灌食方式迫害邓国行。邓国行被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押在郑州新密监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html"><span class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓洪成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">15</span>日中午，深圳市警方前往餐厅调查，手拿李南海、肖兵的照片要求工作人员指认，当天午后邓洪成与深圳维权公民肖兵、沈力、李南海、王威被警方扣押，自此失联；其侄子邓剑峰与同城聚餐公民丁岩、董凌鹏、王军及等得知消息之后前往其住处（深圳市杨美村五巷）寻找，亦遭失联；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其在江西的家属被当地派出所警察查问，且拒绝透露当邓洪成下落及具体情况；后获知，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其叔侄二人被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住，其侄子邓剑锋后被取保候审释放；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，邓洪成被深圳市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓静静<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，邓静静等<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b
