lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邓术梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。邓术梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邓天永：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，汉族，中学学历，籍贯为广东省中山市沙溪镇汇源社区居委会第<span lang="EN-US">40</span>组；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓天玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省荆州市沙市区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，她曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在武汉女子监狱遭受残忍酷刑折磨，双手背铐、用四根绳子吊在房梁上脚尖落地七天七夜，被药物迫害一度精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午十点左右，邓天玉老人在发法轮功资料时被沙市区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>抓捕到荆州市沙市区解放派出所，下午五点多钟才回家。邓天玉被监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日又被沙市区解放派出所抓捕，直接送往石首市（县级市）隔离，于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日晚上从石首市转入荆州区第一看守所，关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，家属都不知道到底几时开的庭，几时宣判的。这是邓天玉老太太第三次被判刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓万英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。邓万英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓秀芬<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁顺景妻子。梁顺景<span lang="EN-US">:1961</span>年出生，广东省梅州市梅县区城东镇人，原中国工商银行梅州分行职工，梅州城区江南团结路苏泊尔电器店负责人，法轮功信仰者。因为人谦和、厚道而深受他人好评；又因其与其妻邓秀芬在当地共同承办苏泊尔电器店（主营电器厨器专卖批发），生意上注重诚实守信，随其公司至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底时已有较大发展；但因梁顺景、邓秀芬夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在信仰追求上笃信并积极宣传法轮功，随遭广东省梅州市当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在开车外出讲解宣传法轮功时，被事先蹲坑等候的梅州市梅江区警方及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室人员联合抓走，其家遭查抄，当场搜走法轮功书籍多套、计算机、打印机及银行卡、身份证等个人对象（如）多件，并将其日用汽车也拉走扣留；次日，其妻因血压高达<span lang="EN-US">180/230</span>，让家人暂时接回，其本人则被梅江区警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，关押至梅江区芹黄看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被梅江区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在梅州市梅江区法院开庭审理；虽因该法院违反法定诉讼程序，其辩护律师曾据理要求法院重新开庭审判，但其与其妻仍然被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判；其中，梁顺景被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，其妻邓秀芬被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并各处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，经广东省梅州市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其妻邓秀芬刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；据悉，其在看守所时被查出身体长有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个肿瘤，在被庭审时其辩护权及辩护律师执业权被剥夺；其承办的苏泊尔电器店因长时无人经营，故被迫关门。目前在广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱（广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘镇<span lang="EN-US">/</span>广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓玉林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。邓玉林刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪克坦开（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南州夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人。藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。次成嘉措、迪克坦开两位拉卜楞寺僧人因与<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在夏河县发生的大规模僧俗民众的抗议游行，随后被抓捕。次成嘉措被认为是带头抗议者，在当局对抗议藏人展开大逮捕后出逃，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日于舟曲县遭捕。迪克坦开也于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪力夏提·吾力拜依：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US"> Dilshat Oralbai</span>，穆斯林，曾先后任新疆伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等，哈萨克斯坦国创办企业总负责人，著名新疆媒体人，中国在押良心犯。 自<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年大学毕业起至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后在伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社工作，担任记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等职务；曾翻译出版、发行<span lang="EN-US">15</span>部文学书籍（含儒勒·凡尔纳的《格兰特船长的儿女》等）、<span lang="EN-US">30</span>余本短篇小说（如《自由》等）及<span lang="EN-US">3</span>部电视剧等，并有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多篇文章在新疆地区多次获奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾到国外创业，并在哈萨克斯坦国开办企业，自认企业负责人，创办生产塑料窗框和房门的工厂；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，因听从中共新疆政府要求在外哈萨克族人必须回国，遂与两个妹妹纷纷返回国内；起初两年生活安然如常，<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，迪力夏提·吾力拜依与两个妹妹突然被伊犁州奎屯市警方以不知名罪由抓捕，并送某政治再教育转化营关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家属接到警方口头通知，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院以不确罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，其两个妹妹亦遭同等命运，大妹被判<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，小妹被判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年； 据悉，其因曾做过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次手术，身体极度虚弱需要及时服药，但在狱中却遭虐待，狱方不仅让其从早到晚不停工作，且拒绝对其进行应有的基本治疗；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2043</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。目前在新疆生产建设兵团农七师奎屯监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">丁汉忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，山东省潍坊市昌乐县乔官镇丁家山村村民，退伍军人，抗暴维权者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年因其住宅遭强拆而引发房屋权属争议，双方未达成拆迁安置补偿协议，后其房屋虽被当局非法偷拆和强拆过两次，但因其誓死捍卫，屡次报警，并到镇县政府多次反映逼拆问题而终使家园得以保全，遂引起当地官员的极端仇视。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日其房屋被进行第三次强拆，因来势凶猛，言行蛮横恶劣，差点使其和家人被砸在屋内，随引起冲突，其全家遭暴打群殴，其头颅前部被拆迁方严重铲伤，当即血流如注，头昏眼花。其曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次报警，但警方却迟迟未到，情急之下其被迫自卫，致使<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名暴力拆迁者受伤，后经抢救无效死亡。其亦因头部伤势过重被送进医院抢救，但很快被赶来的昌乐县警方逮捕。审讯期间，惨遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其被山东潍坊中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥权终身。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日经山东省高院二审，要求撤销一审判决，发回重审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再审，最终被以“故意杀人罪”改判为死缓。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。目前被羁押在潍坊市昌乐县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁家喜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京航空航天大学获得工学学士和工学硕士（飞机制造专业）。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>至<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年在沈阳航空工业总公司、北京航空工业总公司任工程师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起转为专职律师，任职于北京市多家律师事务所。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年参与设立北京市德鸿律师事务所任高级合伙人。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起积极参与推动“随迁子女就地高考”教育平权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日与许志永等人发表致习近平等中共高层领导人公开信，要求包括习近平在内的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名中国部级以上官员率先财产公示。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日丁家喜被当局以“非法集会”罪名刑事拘留，关押在北京市第三看守所。同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，公安机关将丁家喜罪名更换为“寻衅滋事”提交检察院。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日北京市检察院一分院将案件退回公安局补充侦查，控罪更换为“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，北京市海淀区法院判处丁家喜有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日丁家喜刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，北京人权律师丁家喜在朋友家中被山东国保警察带走，手机等物品被查抄。所涉理由不明。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师接到临沂市检察院电话：丁、许二案均第二次退回公安补充侦查。丁家喜现关押在山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。丁雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丁燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：丁燕被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西公民，网名“南柯舟”。自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日发出消息称被警方控制在医院，被逼删除推文，此后失联至今，情况不明。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，董斌在第一时间确认泼墨女孩董瑶琼的身份，并提供其个人、家庭信息，于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被山西国保以“利用手机、电脑使用境外推特软件声援泼墨行动，扰乱公共秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，董斌在得知董瑶琼被送入精神病院后，在推特上发起了拯救董瑶琼的联署行动，于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕，山西当局以“在社交软件上发表不实言论，散布谣言，扰乱公共秩序罪”将其再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，董斌被正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，他被忻府区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月监禁，并被强制删除全部推文。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，董斌出狱。他顶着压力上推特，控诉在狱中曾遭受的酷刑。当局对他的严密监，派出所治安员紧盯，不许离家，他连看病就医的自由也被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，董斌在推特发文，控诉当局对他限制出境。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，董斌再在推特发文呼吁勿忘被关精神病院的董瑶琼，在新年到来之际给她写贺年信件。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，他发出的最后一条消息：“被公安政府五人以上困在医院，逼我删除全部推文”，此后一直失联。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，推特账号<span lang="EN-US"> @realNankezhou </span>显示被冻结。一直处于强迫失踪状态，毫无音信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董勇勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><a name="_Hlk52021054"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董维兴：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52021054;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省四平市伊通县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，四平市伊通县教师进修学校教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，董维兴被伊通县公安局国保警察抓捕，被关押在伊通县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，董维兴被伊通县法院庭审；四月初获悉，董维兴被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52021054;"></span> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董瑶琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南泼墨女。董瑶琼<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初被第三度关进株洲市第三精神病院。长期关注董瑶琼的北京画家华涌是在<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在推特首先发布了这个消息。而董瑶琼的推特内容基本已经被清空。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月董瑶琼向中共总书记习近平的头像上泼墨，之后被上海公安拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被当局送回老家湖南省株洲市攸县，并以疑有精神病为由，将董瑶琼先后两次关进株洲市医院。董瑶琼在被拘押期间，饱受酷刑虐待。其父董建彪告诉媒体，女儿在关押期间曾被强迫吃药。董瑶琼在获释时，呈现出与原先活泼开朗的样子截然不同的模样。获释后的董瑶琼，变成沉默寡言、神情紧张，甚至是有些痴呆的样子。董瑶琼去年获释后在推特发视频称，当地政府要求她上班，以便于监视。她在视频中强调自己没有精神病，是当局强制把她关入精神病院。后来该推文被删除。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月出生。鄠邑区两名法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元，枉判刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董云仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省文山市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>十日早上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，董云仙老人在文山市下沙坝农贸市场住宿楼发法轮功资料时，被抓捕，带到文山市卧龙派出所。后被刑事拘留、批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在砚山县看守所，被文山市法院视频开庭、，对董云仙老人判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜贺先：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北雄县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，杜贺先被雄县公安局国保警察抓捕。后杜贺先被保定市中院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被从保定看守所转到石家庄女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜金花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海维权人士。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜金花原住在上海市浦东新区机场镇。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，由于上海浦东国际机场二期项目，杜金花成了受害者、被拆迁人、失地农民。杜金花上访维权<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多年来未得到安置房子和补偿。多次去北京举报控告，至今没有相关部门解决问题。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10</span>时左右，浦东新区杜金花在家里做中饭，突然被上海市公安局浦东分局川沙派出所警察没有任何法律手续强制带到川沙派出所，被构陷“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在浦东新区看守所。目前案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜景义</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：吉林长春市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年六十多岁，职业是律师，居住在长春市绿园区，一九九六年修炼法轮大。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午，杜景义及妻子崔玉秋和女儿一家三人被抓捕。晚上十一点左右，杜的妻子和女儿被放回。杜景义律师于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被长春市朝阳区法院庭审，杜景义为自己作了无罪辩护<span lang="EN-US">.</span>后杜景义律师被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，没有通知家属，上诉被中级法院驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜全村：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省庆云县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，山东省庆云县公安局国保大队纠集几十个警察，抓捕了正在学习法轮大法著作的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多名法轮功学员。根据长期电话监听和监控，警察又抓捕<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，共计<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，其中大多数是<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的老人，大部份法轮功学员被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，在庆云县法院，夏津县法院人员对六名仍被关押的庆云法轮功学员，赵俊香、王素娟、杜全村、段桂霞、于炳兰、张连云庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东夏津县法院开出判决书：赵俊香判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，杜全村判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王素娟判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于炳兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，张连云判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。杜全村刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川成都市金牛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵正在友人毛坤家做客休息，被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，毛坤、杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑，杜荣判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜晓静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东庆云县法轮功学员，杜晓静是被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的杜全村的女儿。杜晓静在无棣县一餐馆打工，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底给到饭馆吃饭顾客讲真相，被顾客恶告，无棣县公安局警察将杜晓静抓捕，直接关押到德州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜以合：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省临沂市沂南县法轮功学员，杜以合<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十六岁，家住沂南县苏村镇东菜园村，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“青岛峰会”前，他从外地打工回家，沂南公安局和苏村派出所警察多次上门骚扰他的正常生活，不允许他出去打工。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日“为防止他外出打工”，警察入室抓捕了他。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沂南法院在沂南看守所秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在山东省济南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段守珍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：武汉市青山区人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功被长期监控和受到打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，当其在武汉市汉口区金家墩邮局附近宣传法轮功时，遭到青山区公安分局郑珂的构陷，随被武汉市汉口区警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月其案件被转至武汉市青山区检察院。期间因证据不足，青山区检察院两次退侦，要求补充资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日其案件已转至武汉市青山区法院，武汉市青山区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日庭审，至今刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段天俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽合肥市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，段天俊陪妻子去拿药（他妻子是几年前段天俊被迫害时惊吓过度造成精神出现问题），被合肥市滨湖派出所便衣跟踪抓捕，后强行闯入家中非法抄家。段天俊之妻潘能存虽未修炼法轮功，也被指控：因为陪伴丈夫段天俊外出时，段天俊发了救人真相传单，而被拘役六个月，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。而段天俊被合肥市蜀山区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，之前因其已被羁押过一年九个月，故刑期为：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日～</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段宜法：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。家住佳木斯市向阳区红旗路北段林机小区红旗佳苑，户籍所在地是佳木斯市郊区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，佳木斯市向阳公安分局松林派出所片八个警察闯入段宜法家实施抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">后被关押在佳木斯市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年末被庭审，后得知段宜法遭判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨著名商人、民营企业家、神湖集团创办人多吉扎西于<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被不公开审判，判处无期徒刑。</b>现西藏自治区法院给多吉扎西定的罪名是“贷款诈骗罪”，然而，该案疑点是，涉案金额仅仅<span lang="EN-US">150</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，北京法律界专家论证结果是，多吉扎西无法认定犯有贷款诈骗罪，仅仅犯挪用资金罪。并建议西藏自治区法院改判有期徒刑。据了解，多吉扎西在狱中坚持不认罪，一直苦苦等待冤案平反，而多吉扎西的哥哥因多次为弟上访，已被西藏维稳部门禁止离开拉萨市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年多吉扎西的亲人已聘请北京泽博律师事务所的王飞律师为其辩护。王飞前往拉萨后，在多次请求下，终于获得监狱方面探视机会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多杰扎才（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达塘乡央唐区<span lang="EN-US">4</span>村人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌多项罪名正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被以拉萨市中级法院以“阻止政府在‘纳拉赞巴’圣上开矿”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，以“私下向他人贷款罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，以“妨碍公务罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。目前被关押在拉萨扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">E.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">F.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范明兰、范士荣、<span style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">范伟、范文成、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范香芹</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">范一平、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范志刚、</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">方斌、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方宗菊、房彩云</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯际梅、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯及英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯立齐</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、冯群豪、冯少勇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯淑杰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、冯小妹、冯蕴青、丰晓燕、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付秋荣、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付瑞英、付淑贤</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">付文花、傅炫娟、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付燕飞</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙民主人士，网名铁子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四”前夕被刑拘，被捕原因与其长期从事墙外信息搬运工作有关，其本人创建的微信公民群及<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，群友一度达到两三千人，目前猜测当局可能担忧其“六四”有所动作而将其刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁的樊钧益早年曾组织、参与多种公益活动，包括关爱山区学童、定时组织探望敬老院老人及参与公益百公里志愿者活动等，系一名忠实的“中国国民党”粉丝，并自称该党“精神党员”。长期坚持利用翻墙软件了解国际媒体报道，并将消息转发至墙内，在由其创建的微信群和<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传发，亦曾多处组织参与举牌活动，并因此被警方多次拘留处罚。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范明兰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省延吉市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功，因坚持信仰<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。后被数次抓捕，曾遭酷刑折磨。范明兰<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右又被延边州龙井市警察抓捕，七月末家人获悉，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范士荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。法轮功学员，医生。本在广东省潮州市饶平县康民医院工作，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警方绑架，目前被非法关押浙江丽水看守所。看守所不允许她看医生，疫情期间不允许亲友存衣物，不允许律师会见，家属给存的钱也不让花。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，范士荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">范伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁本溪市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，到西湖区彩北派出所，跟警察讲法轮功，结果，范伟被警察抓捕，后又被转至本溪市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，他被本溪市南芬区法院视频开庭，并判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E4%BF%AE%E7%82%BC%E5%A4%A7%E6%B3%95%E4%BB%85%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%9C%AC%E6%BA%AA%E5%B8%8263%E5%B2%81%E8%8C%83%E4%BC%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-434263.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范文成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常居广东省广州市，原广州市某房地产中介商，广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕受害人，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，虽经常参与民主维权活动及与民主友人在一起的聚餐活动，但因其为人处事低调，故而一直鲜为人知；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当其与民主友人胡天峰为谋生计正忙于筹备合伙成立一所保安公司之时，突然与民主公民范一平、胡天峰等多人被广东省广州市国安局以“颠覆国家政权”为由抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，知其又被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”予以正式逮捕，另有范一平等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人亦被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被广州市国安局移送至广州市检察院审查起诉；据悉，其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被抓捕皆可能与他们多次一起聚餐闲聊时，谈论了政治敏感话题有关；目前被羁押于广州市安全局看守所（广州市花都区迎宾大道<span lang="EN-US">111</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510800</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/1112_10.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/1112_10.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">范香芹</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河南省安阳市内黄县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份，内黄县田氏乡法轮功学员范香芹在家被警察抄家抓捕；内黄县张龙乡西张龙村法轮功学员房彩云在家被警察抓捕，她俩一直被关押在安阳市看守所。后房彩云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，范香芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。范香芹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434312.html#21122224724-2"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434312.html#21122224724-2</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范一平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">自民主墙以来的老民运，资深民主人权捍卫者。广东省广州市人，中共干部家庭出身，曾就读于军医大学，毕业后任外科医生，后转行成为某食品贸易公司经营者，房地产中介小商人，成功珠宝商，中国在押政治犯。自民主墙时期就参与民主运动，多年来一直致力于推动中国社会的人权及法治进步事业，故长期受到当局监控和敏感时期被限制人身自由；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年末，曾因接待秘密回国推动民主运动的中国异议人士王炳章，并帮助另一位异见人士王希哲逃往美国，而被中共广东当局判刑入狱三年；出狱后，因继续持守民主理念和抗争，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年六四前夕，曾再次被广州警方以“寻衅滋事” 为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其居所遭搜查；因中共最高领导人习近平主政以来，对民主异见人士监控、打压愈加强烈，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其与另四名（范文成、赖见君、乔连红和珠海市的阿龙）民运人士在“广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕”中，被广州市国安局以涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪抄家后带走，据悉次日又被送进医院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被广州市国家安全局以同罪名转为刑事拘留。目前被羁押于广州市国家安全局看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省葫芦岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，范志刚和妻子苏爽被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被葫芦岛市山区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日法院下达的判决书，范志刚被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；苏爽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">方斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉人，公民记者，武汉公民记者方斌被人们誉为“活着的吹哨人”，方斌因为直播武汉疫情于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日晚上被武汉警方强行入户，在没有搜查证的情况下，对其家中电脑、手机扣押。方斌<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日以手机直播的方式去了武汉几家医院，因其在五医院的几分钟时间无意发现殡仪馆运送八具尸体堆放，此视频引起海内外舆论震动。后，方斌在视频上向全世界公开宣示<span lang="EN-US">:</span>号召国人起来全民自救、推翻暴政，开展全民反抗运动。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午遭到武汉警方破门抓捕。至今音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方宗菊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，湖北孝感市安陆市法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功方宗菊曾经被判刑两年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，方宗菊在安陆市区讲法轮功被抓捕，被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被安陆市法院庭审，多日后得知她被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯立齐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：</span>冯立齐<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯群豪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，汉族，初中毕业，住所地为广东省肇庆市四会市东城街道陶冲村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。冯群豪刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯少勇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯淑杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江鸡西虎林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1997</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，虎林市公安局国保大队刘强等多个警察在冯淑杰住宅的院落，将代亚军、冯淑杰夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕。之后又来了数个警察强行入室抄家，抢走了大法书籍、真相资料、电子产品等诸多私人物品。当天，冯淑杰被刑拘，送往鸡西市看守所关押，代亚军被关押在虎林市拘留所<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被密山法院开庭。冯淑杰被诬判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，代亚军被诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。冯淑杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b>信息来源</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E8%99%8E%E6%9E%97%E5%B8%82%E4%BB%A3%E4%BA%9A%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%86%AF%E6%B7%91%E6%9D%B0%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430324.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E8%99%8E%E6%9E%97%E5%B8%82%E4%BB%A3%E4%BA%9A%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%86%AF%E6%B7%91%E6%9D%B0%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430324.html</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯小妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏无锡市滨湖区拆迁受害者冯小妹，因被起诉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被无锡市滨湖区人民法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在无锡市第二看守所。冯小妹因房屋拆迁和家中财物被抢等问题，在当地始终无法解决，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日到北京天安门裸奔维权，被当地公安人员带回后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。在被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被无锡市公安局滨湖分局批准逮捕，在关押期间，冯小妹被两次强迫做精神病鉴定，其家人多次前往交涉无果，之后因为滨湖区雪浪街道要跟冯小妹谈拆迁问题，于是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日将她取保候审释放回家。在取保期间，冯小妹并未进京上访维权，却于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又被滨湖区法院以同样罪名批准逮捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭。后判决讯息全无。</span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯蕴青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丰晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毕业于山东师范大学新闻系，临沂市人大副调研员，副县级。二十多年公职期间因不满现有体制不被提拔，不允出国，不准考取研究生博士职称学历，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被市政府组织黑社会撞断腰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年春天退党退公职，单位拒绝。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月公开支持香港反送中，被送进派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠疫情间对体制内失察渎职，捐款贪污，罔顾人命，胡作非为忍无可忍，故上京发声。却被侮辱为精神病并强制治疗。丰晓燕拒不认罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被送至临沂第四精神病院，北京路育才路派出所二十多位警察，将患有腰椎间盘突出的丰晓燕在水泥地板拖行至住院部三楼，未进行精神检测，强行关进精神病医院。污蔑其为精神分裂症并强制用药。一直关押在精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，广东省深圳市人，“打工者中心劳动力”（<span lang="EN-US">Worker Empowerment</span>）工作人员，劳动法律咨询者，公益维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年始，其所在打工者中心以开展公益事业为己任，每年为至少<span lang="EN-US">500</span>名企业外来打工者提供免费法律咨询，举办超过<span lang="EN-US">200</span>余次免费文娱学习活动，使至少十万名工友受惠，因其亦参与其中，遂倍受基层工友的广泛欢迎；自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年以来，因焊接设备制造商深圳佳士科技<span lang="EN-US">(Jasic Technology)</span>与员工发生劳资冲突，佳士员工愤起维权抗议，其代表“打工者中心”前往调查介入，并与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名佳士工友积极尝试在中国大陆组建工会（类似于欧美国家里专门为工人谋福利的“工会”，而非“中华全国总工会”），遂遭到当局的严厉打击，被深圳警方多次传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，参与组建工会的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名工人因“试图成立非法工会”而被警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘押，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其因在警察局门外喊口号声援被抓工人，故而亦被深圳市坪山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”正式逮捕；据悉，其姐付红娥曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日为其递交“取保候审申请书”遭拒，理由是一旦批准申请，就“可能毁灭、伪造证据，干扰证人作证或者串供”，<span lang="EN-US">2019 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又在深圳市第二看守所给其汇款后被“查无此人”退回，迄今不予释放。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付秋荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省烟台市龙口法轮功学员。袁玉芹、姚新人、付秋荣<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被国保跟踪抓捕。身强力壮的姚新人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，在龙口市张家沟看守所「突发」脑溢血，在龙口市人民医院被做开颅手术和气管切开术，龙口公安安插四五个警察在医院进行二十四小时监视。姚新人成植物人状态。龙口公安、国保、看守所至今没给家属任何解释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，袁玉芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，付秋荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。付秋荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付瑞英<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北唐山市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点钟，唐山丰润区公安局局长刘金良等有计划、有预谋抓捕丰润区法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、付瑞英、尉国申、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺、陆彩芸、韩玉芹、肖慧君等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁的法轮功学员韩玉芹当天被端明路派出所迫害致死。后来，耿福霞、付瑞英、尉国申以不同的病业形式返回家中；王秀红、陆彩芸、钱淑娟、邱瑞旺被转到唐山第一看守所遭受迫害。当时被抓捕的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员被构陷到遵化市法院。河北唐山市遵化法院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日对<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员耿福霞、王秀红、尉国申、付瑞英、陆彩云开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日判付瑞英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><span class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付淑贤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">28</span>日被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，付淑贤被开庭时不让与家人见面，已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现身体状况不正常，不能行走。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436376.html#2212231914-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:
