lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">付文花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖北省南漳县武安镇人，因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月她儿子付学刚遭遇车祸后对方不承担医疗费，交警不予处理让他到法院起诉而上访，上访期间被对此殴打、拘留<span lang="EN-US">,</span>曾在拘留所被迫割腕自尽。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花在京被南漳县武安镇派出所强行押回后被拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，关押在南漳拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午武安镇政府李才明书记和几个不明身份人员强行将付文花从南漳拘留所抬出来塞进车里带走，进行私自拘禁、酷刑虐待并讹诈，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花被折磨至昏死而丢在路旁被人救起。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，付文花被南漳县公安局抓走，关押在湖北省南漳县看守所。付文花于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点在南漳县法院秘密开庭，被以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">傅炫娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，汉族，中专学历，原籍地是广西壮族自治区北海市合浦县常乐镇大教村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付燕飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">长春法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，毕业于东北师范大学生命科学学院本科，是高中教师，于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年毕业前夕开始修炼法轮功，因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚，付燕飞因在劳动公园讲真相，被受中共谎言毒害的人诬告，后被和顺街派出所抓捕，被朝阳区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，付燕飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
</div>
